--- Reading Rules ---
[[[['@gameOver', '==', 'True'], 'and', ['@playerFoodPoints', '<=', '0']], 'or', [['@gameOver', '==', 'False'], 'and', ['@playerFoodPoints', '>', '0']]]]
['(', '(', '(', '@gameOver', '==', 'True', ')', 'and', '(', '@playerFoodPoints', '<=', '0', ')', ')', 'or', '(', '(', '@gameOver', '==', 'False', ')', 'and', '(', '@playerFoodPoints', '>', '0', ')', ')', ')']
['or', 'and', '>', '@playerFoodPoints', '0', '==', '@gameOver', 'False', 'and', '<=', '@playerFoodPoints', '0', '==', '@gameOver', 'True']
======================
[[['@reachedExit', '==', '1'], 'and', ['@playerPos_0', '==', '#exitPos_0'], 'and', ['@playerPos_1', '==', '#exitPos_1']]]
['(', '(', '@reachedExit', '==', '1', ')', 'and', '(', '@playerPos_0', '==', '#exitPos_0', ')', 'and', '(', '@playerPos_1', '==', '#exitPos_1', ')', ')']
['and', 'and', '==', '@playerPos_1', '#exitPos_1', '==', '@playerPos_0', '#exitPos_0', '==', '@reachedExit', '1']
======================
[[[['@reachedExit', '==', '1'], 'and', ['@gameOver', '==', 'False']], 'or', [['not', ['@reachedExit', '==', '1']], 'and', ['@gameOver', '==', 'True']]]]
['(', '(', '(', '@reachedExit', '==', '1', ')', 'and', '(', '@gameOver', '==', 'False', ')', ')', 'or', '(', '(', 'not', '(', '@reachedExit', '==', '1', ')', ')', 'and', '(', '@gameOver', '==', 'True', ')', ')', ')']
['or', 'and', '==', '@gameOver', 'True', 'not', '==', '@reachedExit', '1', 'and', '==', '@gameOver', 'False', '==', '@reachedExit', '1']
======================
[['not', [['@enemy1Pos_0', '==', '#exitPos_0'], 'and', ['@enemy1Pos_1', '==', '#exitPos_1']]]]
['(', 'not', '(', '(', '@enemy1Pos_0', '==', '#exitPos_0', ')', 'and', '(', '@enemy1Pos_1', '==', '#exitPos_1', ')', ')', ')']
['not', 'and', '==', '@enemy1Pos_1', '#exitPos_1', '==', '@enemy1Pos_0', '#exitPos_0']
======================
[['not', [['@playerPos_0', '==', '@enemy1Pos_0'], 'and', ['@playerPos_1', '==', '@enemy1Pos_1']]]]
['(', 'not', '(', '(', '@playerPos_0', '==', '@enemy1Pos_0', ')', 'and', '(', '@playerPos_1', '==', '@enemy1Pos_1', ')', ')', ')']
['not', 'and', '==', '@playerPos_1', '@enemy1Pos_1', '==', '@playerPos_0', '@enemy1Pos_0']
======================
[[['@playerPos_0', '>=', '#boardBounds_0'], 'and', ['@playerPos_0', '<=', '#boardBounds_1'], 'and', ['@playerPos_1', '>=', '#boardBounds_2'], 'and', ['@playerPos_1', '<=', '#boardBounds_3']]]
['(', '(', '@playerPos_0', '>=', '#boardBounds_0', ')', 'and', '(', '@playerPos_0', '<=', '#boardBounds_1', ')', 'and', '(', '@playerPos_1', '>=', '#boardBounds_2', ')', 'and', '(', '@playerPos_1', '<=', '#boardBounds_3', ')', ')']
['and', 'and', 'and', '<=', '@playerPos_1', '#boardBounds_3', '>=', '@playerPos_1', '#boardBounds_2', '<=', '@playerPos_0', '#boardBounds_1', '>=', '@playerPos_0', '#boardBounds_0']
======================
